Legacy.... (Long post)\\n.\\n.\\nI'm truly blessed to have an experience that most don't get to have. It's rare to have the ability to see your father be the sole owner and operator of their business. It's been a gift to be able to watch an industry change, a business evolve which allowed me to grow a curiosity in me to learn more about it and build a genuine love for it. \\n\\nThe most incredible part was to grow up accompanying my father in appointments from a young age and  seeing how he interacts and services his clients and seeing the friendships he has built with them. I think when I look back at those moments that was the deciding factor me: I want to help build out his legacy, expand upon it and meet incredible people to build those relationships with over a lifetime. \\n\\nWhen I joined at the start of the year I couldn't imagine, as with all of us, where the world would be at this time now, but there truly was no a better time to join him and start this new chapter in my life and our lives.
